68a4(5): riM sems kyi ba d du ss te/ rniml 'khong gsim gyi ci' le bchog rmi la bzlogs so/ rgyung khe ls gla o las/ god min la gsang ba'i 'obr steo nye bug sa'o// 
68a5(5): 'tha d ci las kgyi loo'i kgyud cos bya ba s+dzogs po// rgya kar gyi yis ci ma mi rang nang / bod kyi lo tshe ba skubs rkyu na gya ma ras 'gyur ba'o // 
68a6(5): byung iu bu/ ce hyung/ 'nies mtshan dus ggama 'kbyas dge tshogs mthus/ mkhyan lhun grub 'bres par bcas gan gyi/ tshogs s+dzogs kri' byarg gsang / 
68a7(5): chen lam 'di las / myur du nam mkhyen sangs rgyas thob par shog/
